 So why not today let us tell you the love story of the King and Queen of Bhutan
 bhutan, ek aisa desh jo kshetrafal main bhale hi chota ho lekin khush rahane ke maamle main yahaan ke log kai viksit deshon se bhi aage hai
 Jigme Khesar Nagyal Wangchuk assumed the throne in 2008
 padbhaar sanbhaalane ke kuch hi saalon main wo vahaan kii janata ke chahete ban gaye
 People call them with different names
 kuch unhen ke5 kehete hai to kuch ke liye wo prince charming of himalay hai
 Wangchuk is also the youngest throne in the world
 wangchuck or unki patni jetsun pema ke bich 10 saal kaa antar he lekin pyaar ke liye kya umr or kya umr kaa faasla
 You may not believe it, but when Wangchuk was 17 years old and Pema was 7 years old, the two gave heart to each other
 donon kii pehali mulaakaat thimpu main ek family picnic ke dauraan hui thi
 Wangchuk was a prince, not a king at the time, and proposed to Pema with both his knees bent in full royal style
 ye prapojal pyaar ke izhaar kaa nahin tha
 This proposal was a promise to spend life together
 wangchuck ne pema se kaha, jab tum badi ho jaaogi or tab tak agar ham donon hi single rahe to main tumhen apni patni bananaa chaahunga
 Wangchuk, who received a degree in Political Science and Economics from Oxford University, was extremely calm during his school and college days
 unhen dekhakar koi nahin kah saktaa tha ki wo bhi romantic ho sakate hai lekin pema ke aage unhone bhi ghutane tech die
 Wangchuk then moved to Oxford to study and when Pema turned 15, she was sent to London by her parents
 yahi wo vakt tha jab unka pyaar paravaan chadha
 Perhaps you know that being a royal family has to follow many rules and laws, but Wangchuk kept his love away from every rule
 padhai ke dauraan bhivo saarvajanik rup se apane pyaar kaa izhaar karne menziskate nahin the
 After that both of them returned to the country and got married in 2011
 pema apane pati kii hi tarah logon ke bich jaakar unki pareshaaniyaan sunati hai or unki madad karti hai
 You must have noticed that Wangchuk holds his hand whenever he is with his wife
 donon kaa yun haathon main haath thame chalanaa ab bhutan main trend ban chukaa he
 Nobody would have told you these things about the King and Queen of Bhutan: 1
 bhutan ko uske rang-birange textile kaam ke liye janaa jaataa he
 The dress and foot-wear that Pema wore on her wedding day is now the heritage of the textile museum
 2
 Wangchuk and Pema were married in October 2011 and the royal wedding was the biggest media event in Bhutan's history
 3
 While this royal wedding took place in full custom, for the first time in Bhutan's history, a king kissed his queen in public and expressed love
 4
 According to royal obligations in Bhutan, wherever the king goes, his queen will accompany him
 5
 While Bhutan is not prohibited from having more than one wife, Wangchuk has already announced that he will never marry any woman other than Pema
